   179→      display: grid;
   180→      grid-template-columns: 60px 80px 1fr 44px;

   183→    }
   184→    .log-entry:last-child { border-bottom: none; }

   190→    .log-tag {

   195→    }
   196→    .log-tag.auto { background: #1a2a1a; color: #77cc77; }
   197→    .log-tag.use  { background: #1a1a3a; color: #7799ee; }
   198→  </style>
   199→</head>
   200→<body>
   201→  <div id="app">
   202→    <div id="header">
   203→      <h1>AI Aquarium — Debug Dashboard</h1>
   204→      <div id="clock">8:00 AM</div>
   205→    </div>

   211→      <button class="speed-btn active" data-speed="1">1x</button>
   212→      <button class="speed-btn" data-speed="2">2x</button>
   213→      <button class="speed-btn" data-speed="4">4x</button>
   214→      <div class="ctrl-sep"></div>

   223→        </div>

   226→          <div id="characters-grid"></div>
   227→        </div>
   228→      </div>

   230→        <div class="section-title">Event Log</div>
   231→        <div id="event-log"><div style="color:#555;padding:4px 0">No events yet.</div></div>
   232→      </div>

   235→
   236→  <script type="module">
   237→    import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './src/objects.js';
   238→    import { SimulationEngine } from './src/Engine.js';
   239→    import { Character } from './src/Character.js';
   240→
   241→    // ── Walkable grid (mirrors scene.js) ──────────────────────────────────────
   242→
   243→    const GRID_COLS = 19;
   244→    const GRID_ROWS = 13;
   245→
   246→    function buildWalkableGrid() {
   247→      const grid = [];
   248→      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
   249→        const r = [];
   250→        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
   251→          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
   252→        }
   253→        grid.push(r);
   254→      }
   255→      return grid;
   256→    }
   257→
   258→    // ── Character definitions (mirrors scene.js) ─────────────────────────────
   259→
   260→    const CHARS_CONFIG = [
   261→      { name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6,  ty: 7,
   262→        dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?'] },
   263→      { name: 'Lucy',   label: 'Sol',   tx: 10, ty: 6,
   264→        dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'Such peaceful light...'] },
   265→      { name: 'Ash',    label: 'Nyx',   tx: 14, ty: 5,
   266→        dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect'] },
   267→    ];
   268→
   269→    // ── Engine setup ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   270→
   271→    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();
   272→    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS });
   273→
   274→    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {
   275→      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({
   276→        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   277→      }));
   278→    }
   279→
   280→    // ── UI state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   281→
   282→    let paused = false;
   283→    let speed  = 1;
   284→    let lastTs = null;
   285→
   286→    // Event log (newest-first)
   287→    const log = [];
   288→    const MAX_LOG = 150;
   289→    let logDirty = false;
   290→
   291→    // Track previous object states so we can log from→to
   292→    const prevStateMap = new Map();
   293→    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   294→      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   295→    }
   296→
   297→    // ── Controls ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   298→
   299→    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');
   300→    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   301→      paused = !paused;
   302→      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';
   303→      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);
   304→      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume
   305→    });
   306→
   307→    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
   308→      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   309→        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);
   310→        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   311→        btn.classList.add('active');
   312→      });
   313→    });
   314→
   315→    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {
   316→      // Reset object states to defaults
   317→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   318→        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);
   319→        if (!obj) continue;
   320→        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';
   321→        obj._resetAutoTimer();
   322→        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);
   323→      }
   324→      // Reset sim clock
   325→      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
   326→      // Clear log
   327→      log.length = 0;
   328→      logDirty = true;
   329→      // Update badge classes immediately
   330→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   331→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   332→      }
   333→    });
   334→
   335→    // ── Helper: state badge class ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   336→
   337→    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   338→      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',
   339→    ]);
   340→    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);
   341→
   342→    function badgeClass(state) {
   343→      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';
   344→      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';
   345→      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';
   346→      return 'other';
   347→    }
   348→
   349→    // ── Log helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   350→
   351→    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {
   352→      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   353→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   354→      logDirty = true;
   355→    }
   356→
   357→    // ── Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) ─────────────────────
   358→
   359→    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {
   360→      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   361→      if (!obj) return;
   362→      const from = obj.state;
   363→      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   364→      if (ev) {
   365→        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);
   366→        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);
   367→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   368→      }
   369→    };
   370→
   371→    // ── Build DOM cards (once) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   372→
   373→    function initObjectCards() {
   374→      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');
   375→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   376→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   377→        card.className = 'object-card';
   378→        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;
   379→        card.innerHTML = `
   380→          <div class="object-card-header">
   381→            <span class="object-name">${obj.name}</span>
   382→            <span class="state-badge" id="badge-${obj.id}"></span>
   383→          </div>
   384→          <div class="position-hint">tile (${obj.tx}, ${obj.ty})</div>
   385→          <div class="timer-bar" id="timerbar-${obj.id}" style="display:none">
   386→            <div class="timer-fill" id="timerfill-${obj.id}" style="width:0%"></div>
   387→          </div>
   388→          <div class="timer-text" id="timertext-${obj.id}" style="display:none"></div>
   389→          <div class="interactions" id="int-${obj.id}"></div>
   390→        `;
   391→        grid.appendChild(card);
   392→        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint
   393→      }
   394→    }
   395→
   396→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   397→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   398→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   399→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   400→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   401→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   402→      if (!badge) return;
   403→
   404→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   405→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   406→
   407→      if (stateChanged) {
   408→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   409→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   410→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   411→
   412→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   413→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   414→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   415→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   416→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   417→        ).join('');
   418→      }
   419→
   420→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   421→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   422→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   423→      if (hasTimer) {
   424→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   425→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   426→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   427→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   428→        timerText.style.display = '';
   429→        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;
   430→      } else {
   431→        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';
   432→        timerText.style.display = 'none';
   433→      }
   434→    }
   435→
   436→    function initCharacterCards() {
   437→      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');
   438→      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {
   439→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   440→        card.className = 'character-card';
   441→        card.id = `char-${i}`;
   442→        grid.appendChild(card);
   443→        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint
   444→      });
   445→    }
   446→
   447→    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {
   448→      const card = document.getElementById(`char-${i}`);
   449→      if (!card) return;
   450→
   451→      const targetName = char.interactTarget
   452→        ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)
   453→        : char.targetObjectId
   454→          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)
   455→          : '—';
   456→
   457→      card.innerHTML = `
   458→        <div class="character-name">${char.label}</div>
   459→        <div class="char-row">
   460→          <span>Action</span>
   461→          <span class="action-badge ${char.action}">${char.action}</span>
   462→        </div>
   463→        <div class="char-row">
   464→          <span>Position</span>
   465→          <span class="char-value">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>
   466→        </div>
   467→        <div class="char-row">
   468→          <span>Facing</span>
   469→          <span class="char-value">${char.facing}</span>
   470→        </div>
   471→        <div class="char-row">
   472→          <span>Target</span>
   473→          <span class="char-value">${targetName}</span>
   474→        </div>
   475→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   476→          <span>Mood</span>
   477→          <span class="char-value">${char.mood}</span>
   478→        </div>
   479→        <div class="stat-bar">
   480→          <div class="stat-fill mood" style="width:${char.mood}%"></div>
   481→        </div>
   482→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   483→          <span>Energy</span>
   484→          <span class="char-value">${char.energy}</span>
   485→        </div>
   486→        <div class="stat-bar">
   487→          <div class="stat-fill energy" style="width:${char.energy}%"></div>
   488→        </div>
   489→      `;
   490→    }
   491→
   492→    function renderEventLog() {
   493→      if (!logDirty) return;
   494→      logDirty = false;
   495→
   496→      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');
   497→      if (log.length === 0) {
   498→        el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555;padding:4px 0">No events yet.</div>';
   499→        return;
   500→      }
   501→      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => `
   502→        <div class="log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}">
   503→          <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   504→          <span class="log-obj">${e.objectId}</span>
   505→          <span class="log-transition">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>
   506→          <span class="log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}">${e.trigger}</span>
   507→        </div>
   508→      `).join('');
   509→    }
   510→
   511→    // ── Tick loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   512→
   513→    function tick(ts) {
   514→      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   515→
   516→      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {
   517→        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;
   518→
   519→        // Snapshot states before update
   520→        const snap = new Map();
   521→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   522→
   523→        // Advance simulation
   524→        simEngine.update(realDelta);
   525→
   526→        // Detect auto-transitions
   527→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   528→          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {
   529→            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');
   530→            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   531→          }
   532→          updateObjectCard(obj);
   533→        }
   534→
   535→        // Update character cards
   536→        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));
   537→      }
   538→
   539→      lastTs = ts;
   540→
   541→      // Clock
   542→      document.getElementById('clock').textContent = simEngine.getSimTimeString();
   543→
   544→      // Event log (only when dirty)
   545→      renderEventLog();
   546→    }
   547→
   548→    // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   549→
   550→    initObjectCards();
   551→    initCharacterCards();
   552→    requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   553→  </script>
   554→</body>
   555→</html>
   556→

    46→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    47→  const grid = [];
    48→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
    49→    const r = [];
    50→    for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
    51→      r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
    52→    }
    53→    grid.push(r);
    54→  }
    55→  return grid;
    56→}

     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",          // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 }, // for move
    15→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    16→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    17→ */
    18→
    19→export class AIEngine {
    20→  /**
    21→   * @param {object}  [config]
    22→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    23→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    25→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    26→   */
    27→  constructor(config = {}) {
    28→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    29→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    30→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    31→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    32→
    33→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    34→
    35→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    36→    this._timers = new Map();
    37→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    38→    this._pending = new Set();
    39→  }
    40→
    41→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    42→
    43→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    44→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    45→
    46→    for (const char of characters) {
    47→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    48→      t -= deltaMs;
    49→
    50→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name)) {
    51→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    52→        this._requestDecision(char, objects, simState);
    53→      } else {
    54→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    55→      }
    56→    }
    57→  }
    58→
    59→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    60→
    61→  async _requestDecision(character, objects, simState) {
    62→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    63→
    64→    try {
    65→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    66→        .filter(obj => {
    67→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    68→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    69→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    70→        })
    71→        .map(o => ({ id: o.id, label: o.label, state: o.state }));
    72→
    73→      const systemPrompt =
    74→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    75→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    76→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
    77→
    78→      const userPrompt =
    79→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
    80→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
    81→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
    82→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
    83→        `Choose one action:
` +
    84→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
    85→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
    86→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }`;
    87→
    88→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
    89→
    90→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
    91→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
    92→      const body = JSON.stringify({
    93→        model: this.model,
    94→        max_tokens: 256,
    95→        system: systemPrompt,
    96→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
    97→      });
    98→
    99→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   100→
   101→      if (!res.ok) {
   102→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   103→        return;
   104→      }
   105→
   106→      const data = await res.json();
   107→
   108→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   109→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   110→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   111→              ?? null;
   112→
   113→      if (!text) {
   114→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   115→        return;
   116→      }
   117→
   118→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   119→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   120→    } catch (err) {
   121→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   122→    } finally {
   123→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   124→    }
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  _applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState) {
   128→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   129→
   130→    switch (decision.action) {
   131→      case 'move':
   132→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   133→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   134→        }
   135→        break;
   136→
   137→      case 'interact': {
   138→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   139→        if (obj) {
   140→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   141→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   142→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   143→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   144→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   145→          }
   146→        }
   147→        break;
   148→      }
   149→
   150→      case 'idle':
   151→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   152→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   153→        break;
   154→    }
   155→
   156→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   157→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   158→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   159→    }
   160→
   161→    if (decision.description) {
   162→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   163→    }
   164→  }
   165→}

     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→      });
    56→    }
    57→
    58→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    59→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    60→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    61→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    62→    }
    63→
    64→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    65→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    66→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    67→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    68→      }
    69→
    70→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    71→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    72→        this._doWander(char);
    73→      }
    74→
    75→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    76→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    77→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    78→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    79→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    80→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    81→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    82→        }
    83→      }
    84→
    85→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    86→      char.update(deltaMs);
    87→    }
    88→  }
    89→
    90→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    91→
    92→  /**
    93→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
    94→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
    95→   */
    96→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
    97→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(char.targetObjectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
    98→
    99→    if (event) {
   100→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId);
   101→      char.startInteraction(char.targetObjectId, obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000);
   102→
   103→      if (event.speech) {
   104→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   105→      }
   106→
   107→      if (event.emoji) {
   108→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   109→      }
   110→    }
   111→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   112→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   113→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   114→  }
   115→
   116→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   117→
   118→  _doWander(char) {
   119→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   120→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   121→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   122→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   123→        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile
   124→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   125→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   126→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   127→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   128→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   129→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   130→            return;
   131→          }
   132→        }
   133→        // All objects unreachable — fall through to random wander
   134→      }
   135→    }
   136→
   137→    // Random walkable tile
   138→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   139→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   140→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   141→      return;
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   145→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   146→
   147→    let moved = false;
   148→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   149→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   150→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   151→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   152→      if (moved) break;
   153→    }
   154→
   155→    if (!moved) {
   156→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   157→    }
   158→  }
   159→
   160→  /**
   161→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   162→   */
   163→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   164→    const dirs = [
   165→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   166→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   167→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   168→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   169→    ];
   170→    for (const d of dirs) {
   171→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   172→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   173→      }
   174→    }
   175→    return null;
   176→  }
   177→
   178→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   179→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   180→    const tiles = [];
   181→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   182→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   183→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   184→      }
   185→    }
   186→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   187→    return tiles;
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   191→
   192→  getSimTimeString() {
   193→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   194→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   195→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   196→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   197→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   198→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   199→  }
   200→}
   201→

   127→
   128→  _applyDecision(character, decision, objects, simState) {
   129→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   130→
   131→    switch (decision.action) {
   132→      case 'move':
   133→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   134→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   135→        }
   136→        break;
   137→
   138→      case 'interact': {
   139→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   140→        if (obj) {
   141→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   142→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   143→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   144→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   145→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   146→          }
   147→        }
   148→        break;
   149→      }
   150→
   151→      case 'idle':
   152→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   153→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   154→        break;
   155→    }
   156→
   157→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   158→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   159→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   160→    }
   161→
   162→    if (decision.description) {
   163→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   164→    }
   165→
   166→    if (this.onDecision) {
   167→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   168→    }
   169→  }
   170→}
   171→

   251→      const grid = [];

   253→        const r = [];

   336→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {

   338→        if (!obj) continue;
   339→        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';

   348→      // Update badge classes immediately

   351→      }
   352→    });
   353→
   354→    // ── Helper: state badge class ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   355→
   356→    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   357→      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',
   358→    ]);
   359→    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);
   360→
   361→    function badgeClass(state) {
   362→      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';
   363→      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';
   364→      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';
   365→      return 'other';
   366→    }
   367→
   368→    // ── Log helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   369→
   370→    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {
   371→      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   372→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   373→      logDirty = true;
   374→    }
   375→
   376→    function pushAILog(charLabel, action, target, dialogue) {
   377→      log.unshift({ type: 'ai', charLabel, action, target, dialogue, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   378→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;

   421→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   422→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   423→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   424→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   425→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   426→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   427→      if (!badge) return;
   428→
   429→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   430→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   431→
   432→      if (stateChanged) {
   433→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   434→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   435→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   436→
   437→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   438→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   439→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   440→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   441→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   442→        ).join('');
   443→      }
   444→
   445→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   446→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   447→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   448→      if (hasTimer) {
   449→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   450→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   451→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   452→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   453→        timerText.style.display = '';
   454→        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;
   455→      } else {
   456→        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';
   457→        timerText.style.display = 'none';
   458→      }
   459→    }

   492→          </div>

   495→          </div>

   499→      card.innerHTML = `
   500→        <div class="character-name">${char.label}</div>

   502→          <span>Action</span>

* debug.html imports: SimulationEngine, Character, ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS

* /api/llm is a Vercel serverless function that proxies to OpenRouter
